.image-gallery {
  content-visibility: auto;
  contain-intrinsic-size: 1200px; /* 估算该组未渲染时的占位高度 */
  display: grid;
  grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(135px, 1fr));
  gap:2px;
}

.gallery-item {
  position: relative;
  overflow: hidden;
  transition: background-color 0.2s;
  background-color: hsla(var(--mono-hue), var(--mono-saturation), 50%, 0.0);
}

.gallery-item:hover {
  background-color: hsla(var(--mono-hue), var(--mono-saturation), 50%, 0.1);
}

.gallery-item img {
  width: 100%;
  height: auto;
  display: block;
}

.gallery-item .image-name {
  bottom: 0;
  left: 0;
  right: 0;
  background-color: hsla(var(--mono-hue), var(--mono-saturation), 50%, 0.15);
  padding: 5px;
  font-size: 12px;
  text-align: center;
}
</style>
